***истребитель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:истребитель.html>истреби́тель</a> (5709)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истребить.html>истреби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">istrebítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истребитель.html>истреби́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">istrebítelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истребитель.html>истреби́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истребитель.html>истреби́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истребитель.html>истреби́телей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">истреби́тельница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>destroyer, exterminator</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fighter plane</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fighter pilot</li></ol>

***истребить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:истребить.html>истреби́ть</a> (10003)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">истрѣбити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">istrěbiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Morphologically, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треба.html>тре́ба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tréba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истребить.html>истреби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">istrebítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истреблять.html>истребля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to annihilate, to destroy, to eradicate, to exterminate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to reduce to nothing</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искоренить.html>искорени́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">iskorenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истребить.html>истреби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">istrebítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:истрепать.html>истрепа́ть</a> (27580)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ис-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">is-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trepátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истрепать.html>истрепа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">istrepátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">истрёпывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wear to rags, to fray, to tear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:истрепать.html>истрепа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нерв.html>не́рвы</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>istrepátʹ</b> nérvy komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wear out [fray] smb's nerves</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>истукан</a> (17906)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">истуканъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">istukanŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, past passive participle of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">истукати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">istukati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to carve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ту́кать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">túkatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>истука́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">istukán</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истукан.html>истука́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истукан.html>истука́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истукан.html>истука́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>idol, statue
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>истука́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stojátʹ kak <b>istukán</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">stand there like a stuffed dummy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sedentary, insensate person</li></ol>

***истый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:истый.html>и́стый</a> (14301)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">истꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">istyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jistъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истый.html>и́стый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ístyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)и́стее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)и́стей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> real, true, authentic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:истый.html>и́стый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:джентльмен.html>джентльме́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ístyj</b> džentlʹmɛ́n/džentlʹmén</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>true</b> gentleman</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> zealous, devoted</li></ol>

***истязавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:истязать.html>истяза́вший</a> (25939)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истязать.html>истяза́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">istjazávšij</span>)
</p>

***исход.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:исход.html>исхо́д</a> (3813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">isxodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исход.html>исхо́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">isxód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исход.html>исхо́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исход.html>исхо́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исход.html>исхо́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>outcome, issue</li>
<li>Exodus</li>
<li>outlet</li>
<li>way out <i>from situation</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:безысходный.html>безысхо́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bezysxódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исходный.html>исхо́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">isxódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***исходить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходи́ть</a> (2917)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ис-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">is-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">isxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изойти.html>изойти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to issue (from), to come (from), to originate (from), to emanate (from)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откуда.html>отку́да</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходи́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слух.html>слух</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Otkúda <b>isxodíl</b> étot slux?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Where did this rumour come from?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to proceed (from), to base oneself (on))
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гипотеза.html>гипо́тезы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>том</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jésli <b>isxodítʹ</b> iz gipótezy o tom, što</i> ― <span class="e-translation">on the hypothesis that</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:необоснованный.html>необосно́ванных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предположение.html>предположе́ний</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>isxodítʹ</b> iz neobosnóvannyx predpoložénij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to proceed from unfounded assumptions</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходя́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>isxodjá</b> iz étovo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hence</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be drained of, to shed a lot of (blood, tears, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>кро́вью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>isxodítʹ</b> króvʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to become weak through loss of blood</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слеза́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>isxodítʹ</b> slezámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cry one's heart out</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изойти.html>изойти́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izojtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to expire, to come to an end</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">isxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">no imperfective form</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go / walk / stroll all over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>по́ле</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>isxodítʹ</b> vsjó póle</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to walk all over the field</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wear out (one's legs)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>isxodítʹ</b> vse nógi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wear out one's legs (from long walks), to walk till one drops</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:исчезать.html>исчеза́ть</a> (2145)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исчезнуть.html>исче́знуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">isčéznutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исчезать.html>исчеза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">isčezátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исчезнуть.html>исче́знуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disappear, to vanish</li>
<li>to wear off</li></ol>
